Log transports registered by the diagnostics-otel plugin silently never attach to the real logger, so no OTLP log records are emitted. This PR moves the transport registry and the active logger reference to a `globalThis.__openclawLogTransportState` singleton, mirroring the existing pattern used by `__openclawDiagnosticEventsState` in `diagnostic-events.ts`.\\n\\n2. **Add opt-in content capture for OTEL traces** — Adds a `diagnostics.otel.includeContent` config flag (default: `false`) that gates attaching user-facing input/output text to `model.usage` trace spans. When enabled, content is emitted as standard `gen_ai.prompt` / `gen_ai.completion` attributes (primary), with `langfuse.observation.input` / `langfuse.observation.output` as secondary compatibility fields. All content is redacted via `redactSensitiveText` before export.\\n\\n## Why one PR\\n\\nThese are two independent fixes that happen to be small enough to review together (+86/-6 across 8 files). Shipping them separately is also fine — the log transport fix has no dependency on content capture, and vice versa.\\n\\n## Relation to existing PRs and issues\\n\\n### Issues addressed\\n\\n- **#39156** — diagnostics-otel plugin: OTLP log export doesn't work — module isolation between gateway and plugin-sdk\\n- **#44943** — `diagnostics.otel: Unrecognized key: \\\"captureContent\\\"` — this PR adds `includeContent` to the strict Zod schema so the config key is accepted\\n- **#45096** — v3.12 diagnostics-otel plugin only reports system metrics, no LLM call traces/spans — this PR adds `gen_ai.*` semantic convention attributes to `model.usage` spans\\n\\n### Improvements over existing PRs\\n\\n**Log transport fix — compared with #50085, #39163, #24258:**\\n\\nThis PR takes the same approach as #50085 (the strongest of the three) by sharing **both** the transport registry **and** the active logger reference via `globalThis`. PRs #39163 and #24258 only share the `externalTransports` Set but not the logger reference, which leaves the late-registration path broken: if the daemon's logger is already built before the plugin calls `registerLogTransport`, the transport still needs to be attached to the live logger immediately. Without a shared `activeLogger`, `registerLogTransport` reads `loggingState.cachedLogger` which is `null` in the plugin's module instance, so the transport silently never attaches.\\n\\n**Content capture — compared with #36231, #21290, #40254:**\\n\\n- Smaller and more focused than #21290 (5735 lines, 40 files) — this PR takes the incremental approach of extending the existing `model.usage` flow rather than redesigning the span hierarchy\\n- Uses standard `gen_ai.*` attributes as the primary content fields (unlike #36231 which uses Langfuse-specific attrs as primary)\\n- Includes Langfuse compatibility attrs as secondary fields (unlike #21290 which only uses standard attrs)\\n- Does not include unrelated files like `PATCHES.md` (present in #36231)\\n- Covers the same emission site as #36231 (`agent-runner.ts`) with the same gating approach (`cfg.diagnostics?.otel?.includeContent`)\\n\\n### Scope note\\n\\nContent capture in this PR is at the reply layer (`agent-runner.ts`), capturing user-facing input/output text — not raw provider request/response bodies, reasoning internals, or tool call content. This is the only `model.usage` emitter in the current codebase. If other emitters are added, they will need the same `includeContent` gate.\\n\\n## Files changed (8)\\n\\n| File | Change |\\n|---|---|\\n| `src/logging/logger.ts` | `globalThis` singleton for The bundled `node-fetch` version inside `gaxios`'s own `node_modules` is **v3.3.2 (ESM-only)**. manual token wiring, and has no docs for data persistence or config layout. The WebSocket connection silently stalls behind Docker/VPN proxies (half-open sockets), leaving the web UI frozen with no recovery path.\\r\\n\\r\\nSupersedes #17104, #17132, #17179, #21934 (fixes #21914)\\r\\n\\r\\n### Why it matters\\r\\n\\r\\nDocker is the primary deployment path for self-hosters. content):\\n\\n1. **Fix log transport module isolation** — `registerLogTransport` in the plugin SDK operates on a module-scoped `externalTransports` Set and reads `loggingState.cachedLogger`, both of which are isolated from the daemon's copies when the plugin is loaded via jiti. Log transports registered by the diagnostics-otel plugin silently never attach to the real logger, so no OTLP log records are emitted. This PR moves the transport registry and the active logger reference to a `globalThis.__openclawLogTransportState` singleton, mirroring the existing pattern used by `__openclawDiagnosticEventsState` in `diagnostic-events.ts`.\\n\\n2. **Add opt-in content capture for OTEL traces** — Adds a `diagnostics.otel.includeContent` config flag (default: `false`) that gates attaching user-facing input/output text to `model.usage` trace spans. When enabled, content is emitted as standard `gen_ai.prompt` / `gen_ai.completion` attributes (primary), with `langfuse.observation.input` / `langfuse.observation.output` as secondary compatibility fields. All content is redacted via `redactSensitiveText` before export.\\n\\n## Why one PR\\n\\nThese are two independent fixes that happen to be small enough to review together (+86/-6 across 8 files). Shipping them separately is also fine — the log transport fix has no dependency on content capture, and vice versa.\\n\\n## Relation to existing PRs and issues\\n\\n### Issues addressed\\n\\n- **#39156** — diagnostics-otel plugin: OTLP log export doesn't work — module isolation between gateway and plugin-sdk\\n- **#44943** — `diagnostics.otel: Unrecognized key: \\\"captureContent\\\"` — this PR adds `includeContent` to the strict Zod schema so the config key is accepted\\n- **#45096** — v3.12 diagnostics-otel plugin only reports system metrics, no LLM call traces/spans — this PR adds `gen_ai.*` semantic convention attributes to `model.usage` spans\\n\\n### Improvements over existing PRs\\n\\n**Log transport fix — compared with #50085, #39163, #24258:**\\n\\nThis PR takes the same approach as #50085 (the strongest of the three) by sharing **both** the transport registry **and** the active logger reference via `globalThis`. PRs #39163 and #24258 only share the `externalTransports` Set but not the logger reference, which leaves the late-registration path broken: if the daemon's logger is already built before the plugin calls `registerLogTransport`, the transport still needs to be attached to the live logger immediately. Without a shared `activeLogger`, `registerLogTransport` reads `loggingState.cachedLogger` which is `null` in the plugin's module instance, so the transport silently never attaches.\\n\\n**Content capture — compared with #36231, #21290, #40254:**\\n\\n- Smaller and more focused than #21290 (5735 lines, 40 files) — this PR takes the incremental approach of extending the existing `model.usage` flow rather than redesigning the span hierarchy\\n- Uses standard `gen_ai.*` attributes as the primary content fields (unlike #36231 which uses Langfuse-specific attrs as primary)\\n- Includes Langfuse compatibility attrs as secondary fields (unlike #21290 which only uses standard attrs)\\n- Does not include unrelated files like `PATCHES.md` (present in #36231)\\n- Covers the same emission site as #36231 (`agent-runner.ts`) with the same gating approach (`cfg.diagnostics?.otel?.includeContent`)\\n\\n### Scope note\\n\\nContent capture in this PR is at the reply layer (`agent-runner.ts`), capturing user-facing input/output text — not raw provider request/response bodies, reasoning internals, or tool call content. This is the only `model.usage` emitter in the current codebase. If other emitters are added, they will need the same `includeContent` gate.\\n\\n## Files changed (8)\\n\\n| File | Change |\\n|---|---|\\n| `src/logging/logger.ts` | `globalThis` singleton for `DiagnosticUsageEvent` |\\n| `src/auto-reply/reply/agent-runner.ts` | Gated content emission |\\n| `extensions/diagnostics-otel/src/service.ts` | `gen_ai.*` + `langfuse.*` attrs, redacted |\\n\\n## implementation to use with this logic:\\n\\n```ts\\nstatic async #getFetch() {\\n  const hasWindow = typeof window !== 'undefined' \\u0026\\u0026 !!window;\\n  this.#fetch ||= hasWindow\\n    ? window.fetch\\n    : (await import('node-fetch')).default;  // \\u003c-- problem\\n  return this.#fetch;\\n}\\n```\\n\\nOn Node.js (no `window`), it falls back to dynamically importing `node-fetch`. The bundled `node-fetch` version inside `gaxios`'s own `node_modules` is **v3.3.2 (ESM-only)**. When loaded from a CJS bundle context on **Node.js 22+**, this fails with:\\n\\n```\\nTypeError: Cannot convert undefined or null to object\\n  at ModuleWrap.\\u003canonymous\\u003e (node:internal/modules/esm/translators:213:12)\\n```\\n\\nNode.js 18+ ships with a native `globalThis.fetch`, but `gaxios` only checks for `window` (browser), not `globalThis.fetch` (Node.js).\\n\\n## https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/discussions/13528#discussioncomment-15885279\\r\\n\\r\\n### Problem(s)\\r\\n\\r\\nRunning OpenClaw in Docker requires memorizing long `docker compose` commands, manual token wiring, and has no docs for data persistence or config layout. The WebSocket connection silently stalls behind Docker/VPN proxies (half-open sockets), leaving the web UI frozen with no recovery path.\\r\\n\\r\\nSupersedes #17104, #17132, #17179, #21934 (fixes #21914)\\r\\n\\r\\n### Why it matters\\r\\n\\r\\nDocker is the primary deployment path for self-hosters. Silent WebSocket stalls make users think the bot is down when it's running fine — they just need to refresh, but nothing tells them that.\\r\\n\\r\\n### What changed\\r\\n- **ClawDock helpers** (`scripts/clawdock/clawdock-helpers.sh`): 15+ shell functions (`clawdock-start`, `clawdock-update`, `clawdock-dashboard`, `clawdock-config`, etc.) with auto-detection of the OpenClaw project directory, colored output, guided next-step hints, and health-polling restarts.\\r\\n- **ClawDock README** (`scripts/clawdock/README.md`): full docs covering quickstart, command reference, config/secrets layout, env precedence, data \\u0026 backups, and common workflows.\\r\\n- **Tick watchdog** in `GatewayBrowserClient`: tracks server tick events and forces reconnect when ticks stall for 2x the interval — detects half-open sockets that TCP keepalive misses in Docker/VPN environments.\\r\\n- **Auto-reload on event gap**: changed from a passive \\\"refresh recommended\\\" banner to calling `refreshChat()` automatically, so the UI recovers without user intervention.\\r\\n- **Timer leak fix** in `GatewayClient.stop()`: clears `connectTimer` on shutdown, preventing zombie reconnect attempts.\\r\\n- **Moved** `scripts/shell-helpers/` → `scripts/clawdock/` and updated all references (`docs/install/docker.md`, install URLs in the script header).\\r\\n- **What did NOT change (scope boundary):** No changes to the gateway server, Docker Compose files, Dockerfile, or any channel/integration code. The tick watchdog is client-side only — no new server events.\\r\\n\\r\\n## Change Type (select all)\\r\\n\\r\\n- [x] Bug fix\\r\\n- [x] Feature\\r\\n- [ ] Refactor\\r\\n- [x] Docs\\r\\n- [ ] Security hardening\\r\\n- [ ] Chore/infra\\r\\n\\r\\n## Scope (select all touched areas)\\r\\n\\r\\n- [x] Gateway / orchestration\\r\\n- [ ] Skills / tool execution\\r\\n- [ ] Auth / tokens\\r\\n- [ ] Memory / storage\\r\\n- [ ] Integrations\\r\\n- [ ] API / contracts\\r\\n- [x] UI / DX\\r\\n- [ ] CI/CD / infra\\r\\n\\r\\n## Linked Issue/PR\\r\\n\\r\\n- Closes #21914\\r\\n- Related #17104, #17132, #17179, #21934\\r\\n\\r\\n## User-visible / Behavior Changes\\r\\n\\r\\n- New `clawdock-*` shell functions available after sourcing `clawdock-helpers.sh` (install via curl or source from repo)\\r\\n- `clawdock-config` prints all config files with masked secret values (replaces the old `cd ~/.openclaw` behavior)\\r\\n- `clawdock-update` and `clawdock-fix-token` now health-poll the gateway instead of a blind `sleep 5`\\r\\n- `clawdock-rebuild` passes `OPENCLAW_INSTALL_BROWSER` build arg from `.env` (previously undocumented gap)\\r\\n- Web UI auto-reloads chat on event gaps instead of showing a passive \\\"refresh recommended\\\" banner\\r\\n- Web UI auto-reconnects when the WebSocket silently stalls (tick timeout at 2x server tick interval)\\r\\n- Gateway client no longer leaks reconnect timers after `stop()` is called\\r\\n\\r\\n## Security Impact (required)\\r\\n\\r\\n- New permissions/capabilities?
